Includes

#include <grx-3.0.h>

Description

This is a list of the key symbols used by GRX. (They are the same as X11.)

Functions

Types and Values

GRX_KEY_NoSymbol

#define GRX_KEY_NoSymbol                    0x000000  /* Special KeySym */

GRX_KEY_VoidSymbol
